# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
Trees ^j6amnZDW

- Tree data structure is a hierarchical structure that is used to represent 
  and organize data in a way that is easy to navigate and search. It is a 
  collection of nodes that are connected by edges and has a hierarchical 
  relationship between the nodes.  ^EfVsEye3

Why?
-> Add, remove & find in O(log(n)) time.
-> Ordered storage (insertion and deletion).
-> Cost effective (dynamic in nature). ^l80p6673

Binary tree : 
-> Hierarchical data structure.
-> Parent node has 2 child nodes.
-> Should be balanced to give log(n)
    operational time complexity, else 
    in case of unbalanced binary search 
    tree gives O(n) time complexity.  ^rsMPmpin

- With self-balancing binary tress we can solve the problem of binary tree.
    but binary tree is also inefficient for sorted data. ^P8MNVZ8J

unbalanced 
binary tree ^XAF1FbCS

Where are binary tree's used ?
-> File systems.
-> Data Bases 
-> Algorithms/Networking
-> Math
-> Decision trees 
-> Compression of files - Huffman Coding
-> Heaps, Graphs, etc... ^eardhTXG

Structure :  ^k1cZ3uSr

5 ^BwPa9Yn0

6 ^zju5yvuX

8 ^lIhpp8Z4

14 ^0aTdDIzA

3 ^0lfjeLuP

9 ^WFSgz1Wr

11 ^ZtVfXY3X

15 ^1CwSyd0W

4 ^JD1Og1UL

siblings ^fTrvrI02

lay ^ffzFsQAo

lay ^fsj1yzPA

lay ^2KCYKLz5

Binary tree :
    int value
    Node left
    Node right ^cnkOFFSu

Properties :
- size : number of nodes 
- child & parent
- siblings
- edge
- height : max number of edges b/w 2 nodes
 ^xU6pevDw
